[30;1m182 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m183 | [0m[35m* Bleach's API is simpler.[0m
[30;1m184 | [0m[35m* Bleach's sanitizer allows a map to be provided for ``ALLOWED_ATTRIBUTES``,[0m
[30;1m185 | [0m[35m  giving you a lot more control over sanitizing attributes: you can sanitize[0m
[30;1m186 | [0m[35m  attributes for specific tags, you can sanitize based on value, etc.[0m
[30;1m187 | [0m[35m* Bleach's sanitizer always alphabetizes attributes, but uses an alphabetizer[0m
[30;1m188 | [0m[35m  that works with namespaces — the html5lib one is broken in that regard.[0m
